<Text>While purchasing some clothing items at the Adelanto store on Bartlett Rd., I asked the sales clerk if I could return anything that does not fit and was told that I could as long as the tags were still attached and I kept my receipt. I purchased several items. Only one item did not fit properly, but when I attempted to return it the next day, the clerk, Alexandra, was not there. I spoke to Alix, who said she was the asst mgr and was told that sale items are not returnable. I explained that the store clerk specifically told me the day before that all my purchases were returnable. Alix spoke to her manager, I did not catch her name, and she also denied my return even though I followed the clerk's instructions. No signs were posted in the store that explained any special return policy...or a deviation from their corporate policy.
Later, I phoned Family Dollar corporate office and a recording while you wait on hold explains that they have a 100% satisfaction guarantee and directs the customer to the website for a complete description of the policy.
I took this information back to Family Dollar store in Adelanto, and even provided the corporate phone number and let Alix see the satisfaction guarantee on their website using my phone, but she said her manager would not allow her to accept the return of sale items. She said i needed to discuss it with her store manager.
I live more than 20 minutes away from this store. The shirt i purchased was marked $10, but sold for $6. Nothing on the shirt nor any sign near the clothing racks indicated it was on sale...only after i purchased it did I discover it was marked down.
I phoned Family Dollar and emailed them about this. It has been three weeks and have not received a response.  It was only $6, but if the store manager will not honor corporate policy, and will not empower her asst mgr to follow what is clearly corporate policy or stand by what their employees tell customers...I am leery of spending my money there.

<Review>Pelicana caught my eye, like every other fried chicken shop, but mainly for its advertisement that it's well known in Korea. It seems like this is a common marketing thing for most chains that make it over to the states, so I should have taken that with a grain of salt, as it may be the least memorable Korean fried chicken I've ever had.

We ordered when takeout only was available, so I can't comment on the service too much aside from the friendly cashiers. It didn't seem well organised though to queue customers to go inside and order, almost like we were about to get cut off by every other person that came up. I don't recall any texting system to let you know your order was ready either, which is a bit of a miss for me considering that it takes a while for the food to get ready (presumably prepped and fried per order?), and it's easy to get lost waiting around The Source.

Overall, the chicken was mostly okay. The main flavours that stuck out to me were just *sweet*. We got the extra crispy chicken with original sauce and hot chili; none were spicy at all. My spice tolerance treats everything from Sriracha to Carolina Reapers the same, and this barely scratched Hot Cheetos. Given the takeout and hefty sauce, I can't comment on the crispiness fairly since it was about 20 minutes by the time we got home, although the crispiness held up (just not that "extra" crispy).

Might come back if I was around The Source again, but there's plenty of other options in the area.<//Review><Pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipO27FaHH8eR3-KIAumVAaj-8TOWiBLZKsAc41tL=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOzTiOaonvP83B9wdcw9pVqVxEuc4j2P2YHfj1V=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//Pics><Response>None</Response>< Gmap_id>

My favorite place for Chicken Wings, KFC (Korean Fried Chicken).  Both original and crispy are good. Juicy wings with crunchy skin and not oily. I recommend to get the sauce on the side. <UserId.>116954966513520274415< /UserId.><username>A K<//username><date>1618207142120<//date><rating>5<//rating>< Review>
Such a fantastic gem of a place. Everything is super here and I was really amazed by the great service, attention to detail and the high quality food. No wonder it's so highly rated.

We really enjoyed everything - including the following:

Miso soup - a mildly salty savory broth with seaweed. Served at the start of the meal.

Crunchy salad - also served as an appetizer with a fantastic mildly sweet and creamy dressing. Really delicious.

Sashimi - assorted platter of chefs choice of fresh fish sashimi. Included salmon and a few others. For someone who was trying it for the first time, I really enjoyed it with the wasabi, soya sauce and ginger.

Crunchy dynamite sushi - deep fried tuna sushi with the most delicious sauce and veggies. This was my favourite item on the menu.

The service was quick and friendly. I really liked the small touches like the really beautiful crockery and the orchid on the food.

This is an expensive place but good for occasional visit. Strongly recommend.< /Review>

< Review>
I felt like Japanese food and found Sake Bomb Sushi on DoorDash.

They have an 2-item bento box for $19.99!!
Did Jesus cook this chicken teriyaki!?

I was craving it so ordered it and 30 mins later, I was shocked.

This 2-item bento box will easily serve 2 people.  Huge SABA and two layers of tonkatsu.  You pay a lot, but you do get 1.5-2x of what a normal bay area Japanese restaurant would serve.  I ordered 2 bento boxes thinking I'll eat another later, but this is going to last me for 4-5 meals.  I'm sorry, I made my point about the size.  It's expensive, but value is there.<//Review>

I decided to stop by this location last night while on my way back home in Temecula. Upon arrival, I noticed solicitors walking around the parking lot and by the front door asking for money so be prepared. The store was clean and had what I was looking for. The cashier was nice, but she forgot to hand me one of my bags (which I believe was an honest mistake). By the time I realized I didn't have my items, the store was closed. The following morning, I called the store to speak to a manager and was put on hold for about 10 minutes. The assistant manager was rude when she picked up the phone and while I was trying to tell her about the items I didn't recieve. She took down my information and informed me the manager will give me a call back after he looks at the video. I don't understand why she couldn't just look at the video if she is an assistant manager. Sadly, I didn't get a call back. It was only a few bucks, so I will just take the lost. Check your bags and make sure you have everything before you leave the store, otherwise you will have to jump through hurdles just to get back what you already paid for. This was my first and now last time I will shop here.< /Text>
